SELECT

FROM TPRIPA PA

WHERE PA.IDIPROC = TPRIPROC.IDIPROC) AS AD_NURAM, (CASE WHEN TPRIPROC.CODPARCTERC IS NULL THEN (SELECT CODPARCTERC FROM TPRTXAT TXAT WHERE TXAT.IDIPROC = TPRIPROC.IDIPROC AND IDEFX = 0) ELSE TPRIPROC.CODPARCTERC END) AS CODPARCTERC FROM TPRIPROC /*SQL_92_JOINED_TABLES*/  WHERE (TPRIPROC.IDIPROC = ?)

##ID_529## tempo: 45 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
SELECT TPRIPA.CODPRODPA AS CODPRODPA,TPRIPA.CONCLUIDO AS CONCLUIDO,TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA AS CONTROLEPA,TPRIPA.DTFAB AS DTFAB,TPRIPA.DTVAL AS DTVAL,TPRIPA.IDIPROC AS IDIPROC,TPRIPA.NROLOTE AS NROLOTE,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR AS QTDPRODUZIR,TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL AS QTDPRODUZIR_ORIGINAL, ( SELECT REFERENCIA FROM TGFPRO PRO WHERE CODPROD = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA) AS REFERENCIA, ( 
	SELECT
		  TPRIPA.QTDPRODUZIR - NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) - (CASE
                                                       				WHEN NVL(SUM(NOTA.QTDNEG), 0) > 0 THEN NVL(MAX(APO_PERDA.QTDPERDA), 0)
                                                      				ELSE 0 
                                                      			  END) AS SALDO
	FROM
		TPRIPA IPA
	INNER JOIN TPRIPROC IPROC ON (IPA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC)
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT IDIPROC, ITE.QTDNEG, ITE.CODPROD, ITE.CONTROLE 
		FROM TGFCAB CAB INNER JOIN TGFITE ITE ON (ITE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPRROPE ROPE ON (ROPE.NUNOTA = CAB.NUNOTA)
						INNER JOIN TPROEST OEST ON (OEST.IDEFX = ROPE.IDEFX AND OEST.SEQOPER = ROPE.SEQOPER)
		WHERE CAB.IDIPROC IS NOT NULL 
			AND OEST.TIPOITENS = 'PA'
			AND OEST.QUANDO = 'PA'
			AND CAB.TIPMOV = 'F'
	) NOTA ON (NOTA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND NOTA.CODPROD = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(NOTA.CONTROLE, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	LEFT JOIN (
		SELECT  NVL(SUM(APA.QTDPERDA), 0) AS QTDPERDA , IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
   		FROM TPRAPA APA
   		INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON(APO.NUAPO = APA.NUAPO)
   		INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON(IATV.IDIATV = APO.IDIATV)
   		WHERE APO.SITUACAO = 'C'
   			AND APA.QTDPERDA > 0
		GROUP BY IATV.IDIPROC, APA.CODPRODPA, APA.CONTROLEPA
	) APO_PERDA ON (APO_PERDA.IDIPROC = IPROC.IDIPROC AND APO_PERDA.CODPRODPA = IPA.CODPRODPA AND (NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' ' OR NVL(APO_PERDA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ')))
	WHERE IPA.CODPRODPA = TPRIPA.CODPRODPA
		AND NVL(IPA.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = TPRIPA.CONTROLEPA
		AND IPROC.STATUSPROC IN ('A', 'R', 'P2', 'S', 'S2')
		AND IPROC.IDIPROC = TPRIPA.IDIPROC) AS SALDOOP FROM TPRIPA /*SQL_92_JOINED_TABLES*/   WHERE (TPRIPA.IDIPROC = ?) 
Params:
  1 = 12356
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

##ID_534## tempo: 4 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
SELECT 
X.CODPRODMP,
X.CONTROLEMP,
SUM(X.QTDMISTURA) AS QTDMISTURA,
X.PROPMPFIXA,
X.CODVOL
 ,X.CODLOCALORIG,
X.TIPOUSOMP,
X.FIXAQTDAPO,
X.TIPOQTD,
X.VINCULOSERIEPA 
FROM(
	SELECT
	LMP.CODPRODMP,
	(CASE 
	WHEN LMP.TIPOCONTROLEMP = 'L' 
		THEN LMP.CONTROLEMP
	WHEN LMP.TIPOCONTROLEMP = 'H'    
		THEN ?
	ELSE 
		' '	
	END
	) AS CONTROLEMP,
	(CASE WHEN LMP.TIPOQTD = 'V' THEN LMP.QTDMISTURA * ? ELSE LMP.QTDMISTURA END) AS QTDMISTURA,
	LMP.PROPMPFIXA,
	NVL(LMP.CODVOL, PRO.CODVOL) AS CODVOL
	 ,LMP.CODLOCALORIG, 
	LMP.TIPOUSOMP,
	LMP.FIXAQTDAPO,
	LMP.TIPOQTD,
	NVL(LMP.VINCULOSERIEPA,'N') AS VINCULOSERIEPA 
	FROM TPRLMP LMP
	INNER JOIN TPREFX EFX ON(EFX.IDEFX = LMP.IDEFX)
	INNER JOIN TPRATV ATV ON(ATV.IDEFX = LMP.IDEFX)
	INNER JOIN TGFPRO PRO ON (PRO.CODPROD = LMP.CODPRODMP )
	WHERE
	EFX.IDPROC = ?
	AND ((? = 0 AND ATV.LISTAMPPADRAO = 'S') OR (? > 0 AND ATV.IDEFX = ?))
	AND (? = 'T' OR LMP.GERAREQUISICAO = ?)
	AND LMP.CODPRODPA = ?
	 AND (LMP.TIPOUSOMP IN ('N'))  
	--TIPO_MATERIAL AND 
	AND (
		(NVL(LMP.CONTROLEPA,' ') <> ' ' AND NVL(LMP.CONTROLEPA,' ') = ?)
		OR (
		NVL(LMP.CONTROLEPA, ' ') = ' '
		AND NOT EXISTS(
			SELECT 1 
			FROM TPRLMP LMP2 
			WHERE
			LMP2.IDEFX = LMP.IDEFX
			AND LMP2.CODPRODPA = LMP.CODPRODPA
			AND NVL(LMP2.CONTROLEPA,' ') = ?
			AND LMP2.CODPRODMP = LMP.CODPRODMP
			AND LMP2.CONTROLEMP = LMP.CONTROLEMP
			AND LMP2.SEQMP <> LMP.SEQMP
			)
		)
	)
) X
GROUP BY X.CODPRODMP,X.PROPMPFIXA,X.CONTROLEMP,X.CODVOL ,X.CODLOCALORIG,X.TIPOUSOMP,X.FIXAQTDAPO,X.TIPOQTD,X.VINCULOSERIEPA 
Params:
  1 =  
  2 = 160
  3 = 30
  4 = 0
  5 = 0
  6 = 0
  7 = T
  8 = T
  9 = 4
  10 =  
  11 =  
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_535## tempo: 3 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr

 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA

  2 = PRODUTO

##ID_539## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO

AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ? ##ID_543## tempo: 0 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr

 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO

##ID_544## tempo: 1 (ms)

 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA

/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5

uri: /mge/service.sbr

 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO

 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA

##ID_551## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO

##ID_552## tempo: 0 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA

  1 = 0
  2 = GRUPO DE PRODUTO

##ID_555## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO

##ID_556## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA

##ID_559## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = PRODUTO
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
##ID_560## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.CODINSTPRINC, REG.TIPO FROM TGFITR ITR   INNER JOIN TGFREG REG ON (REG.CODREGRA = ITR.CODREGRA)   INNER JOIN TGFCER CER ON (CER.CODREGRA = REG.CODREGRA) WHERE   CER.TIPO = 'U'    AND CER.ATIVO = 'S'    AND ITR.ATIVO = 'S'    AND CER.CHAVE = ?    AND TRANSLATE(UPPER(REG.INSTPRINC),'\C1\C9\CD\D3\DA\C3\D5\C2\CA\CE\D4\DB\C0\C8\CC\D2\D9\C7','AEIOUAOAEIOUAEIOUC') = ?   AND CER.FILTRAR = 'S'    AND (REG.INSTSEC IS NULL OR REG.INSTSEC = '')  ORDER BY ITR.CODREGRA,ITR.SEQUENCIA
Params:
  1 = 0
  2 = GRUPO DE PRODUTO

##ID_563## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
SELECT DISTINCT X.CODPRODMPALT, 
                X.QTD_SUB, 
                X.QTDMISTURA, 
                X.QTD, 
                X.CONJUNTO, 
                X.CONTROLEMPALT, 
                X.CODVOL,
                X.ORDEM,
                X.CODLOCALORIG,
                X.CODLOCALBAIXA
FROM   (SELECT DISTINCT MPA.CODPRODMPALT, 
                        IMPA.QTDMISTURA / MPA.QTDMISTURA AS QTD_SUB, 
                        IMPA.QTDMISTURA, 
                        MPA.QTDMISTURA AS QTD, 
                        MPA.CONJUNTO, 
                        MPA.CONTROLEMPALT, 
                        MPA.CODVOL, 
                        IMPA.ORDEM ,
                        MPA.CODLOCALORIG,
                        MPA.CODLOCALBAIXA
        FROM   TPRMPA MPA 
               INNER JOIN TPRIMPA IMPA 
                       ON ( MPA.CODPRODPA = IMPA.CODPRODPA

##ID_589## tempo: 1 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
SELECT
 OPC.NUCAMPO,
 NULL AS NOMECAMPO,
 NULL AS DESCRCAMPO,
 NULL AS LABEL,
 NULL AS ADICIONAL,
 VALOR AS CHAVE,
 OPCAO AS VALOR,
 OPC.ORDEM,
 'O' AS TIPO,
 NULL AS CALCULADO,
 NULL AS PERMITEPADRAO,
 NULL AS APRESENTACAO,
 NULL AS PERMITEPESQUISA,
 NULL AS TIPCAMPO,
 NULL AS VISIVELGRIDPESQUISA
FROM
 TDDOPC OPC
WHERE
 EXISTS(
     SELECT 1 FROM TDDCAM CAM WHERE CAM.NUCAMPO = OPC.NUCAMPO AND CAM.NOMETAB = ?  
 )
UNION ALL
SELECT
 PCO.NUCAMPO,
 NULL AS NOMECAMPO,
 NULL AS DESCRCAMPO,
 CASE
    WHEN NOME = 'labelParam' THEN
	   GET_TSIPAR_TIPO_CT(VALOR)
 END AS LABEL,
 NULL AS ADICIONAL,
 NOME AS CHAVE,
  VALOR, 
 
 NULL AS ORDEM,
 'P' AS TIPO,
 NULL AS CALCULADO,
 NULL AS PERMITEPADRAO,
 NULL AS APRESENTACAO,
 NULL AS PERMITEPESQUISA,
 NULL AS TIPCAMPO,
 NULL AS VISIVELGRIDPESQUISA
FROM
 TDDPCO PCO
WHERE
 EXISTS(
     SELECT 1 FROM TDDCAM CAM WHERE CAM.NUCAMPO = PCO.NUCAMPO AND CAM.NOMETAB = ?  
 )
UNION ALL
SELECT
 NUCAMPO,
 NOMECAMPO,
 DESCRCAMPO,
 NULL AS LABEL,
 ADICIONAL,
 NULL AS CHAVE,
 NULL AS VALOR,
 CAM.ORDEM AS ORDEM,
 'C' AS TIPO,
 CALCULADO,
 PERMITEPADRAO,
 APRESENTACAO,
 PERMITEPESQUISA,
 TIPCAMPO,
 VISIVELGRIDPESQUISA
FROM
 TDDCAM CAM
WHERE
 NOMETAB = ?
  
ORDER BY 1,9,8

  1 = TPRAMP
  2 = TPRAMP
  3 = TPRAMP

##ID_622## tempo: 139 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

  2 = 0
  3 = 12356
  4 = 6

##ID_624## tempo: 2 (ms)

SELECT
	IPROC.IDIPROC,
	IATV.IDIATV,
	APA.CODPRODPA,
	APA.CONTROLEPA,
	PROMP.USALOCAL,
	PROPA.TIPCONTEST AS TIPCONTESTPA,
	PROMP.TIPCONTEST AS TIPCONTESTMP,
	OEST.CODLOCALBAIXAMP 
FROM
	TPRIPROC IPROC
INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON
	(IPROC.IDIPROC = IATV.IDIPROC)
INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON
	(APO.IDIATV = IATV.IDIATV)
INNER JOIN TPRAPA APA ON
	(APA.NUAPO = APO.NUAPO)
INNER JOIN TGFPRO PROMP ON
	(PROMP.CODPROD = ?)
INNER JOIN TGFPRO PROPA ON
	(PROPA.CODPROD = APA.CODPRODPA)
LEFT JOIN TPROEST OEST ON
	(OEST.IDEFX  IN (SELECT IDEFX FROM TPRATV WHERE IDPROC = IPROC.IDPROC))
WHERE
	APO.NUAPO = ?
	AND APA.SEQAPA = ?

THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

##ID_697## tempo: 3 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao

*/
 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

##ID_699## tempo: 2 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao

entity: ApontamentoPA

*/
SELECT
	IPROC.IDIPROC,
	IATV.IDIATV,
	APA.CODPRODPA,
	APA.CONTROLEPA,
	PROMP.USALOCAL,
	PROPA.TIPCONTEST AS TIPCONTESTPA,
	PROMP.TIPCONTEST AS TIPCONTESTMP,
	OEST.CODLOCALBAIXAMP 
FROM
	TPRIPROC IPROC
INNER JOIN TPRIATV IATV ON
	(IPROC.IDIPROC = IATV.IDIPROC)
INNER JOIN TPRAPO APO ON
	(APO.IDIATV = IATV.IDIATV)
INNER JOIN TPRAPA APA ON
	(APA.NUAPO = APO.NUAPO)
INNER JOIN TGFPRO PROMP ON
	(PROMP.CODPROD = ?)
INNER JOIN TGFPRO PROPA ON
	(PROPA.CODPROD = APA.CODPRODPA)
LEFT JOIN TPROEST OEST ON
	(OEST.IDEFX  IN (SELECT IDEFX FROM TPRATV WHERE IDPROC = IPROC.IDPROC))
WHERE
	APO.NUAPO = ?
	AND APA.SEQAPA = ?

##ID_721## tempo: 3 (ms)
/* Runtime-info
Application: OperacaoProducao
Referer: https://satis2.nuvemdatacom.com.br:8110/mgeprod/OperacaoProducao.xhtml5
ResourceID: br.com.sankhya.producao.cad.OperacaoProducao
entity: ApontamentoPA
service-name: DatasetSP.save
uri: /mge/service.sbr
*/
 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC

 SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN (TPRIATV.IDEFX = ? OR ? = 0) THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  UNION  SELECT TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL AS DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX AS IDEFX,  	   SUM(CASE WHEN TPRIATV.IDEFX != ? THEN TGFITE.QTDNEG ELSE 0 END) AS QTDNEG  	FROM TGFITE INNER JOIN TGFCAB ON (TGFITE.NUNOTA = TGFCAB.NUNOTA) 					INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT CODPROD, CONTROLE, DTVAL FROM TGFEST) TGFEST ON (TGFEST.CODPROD = TGFITE.CODPROD AND TGFEST.CONTROLE = TGFITE.CONTROLE) 					INNER JOIN TPRROPE ON TGFCAB.NUNOTA = TPRROPE.NUNOTA 					INNER JOIN TPRIATV ON (TPRIATV.IDIATV = TPRROPE.IDIATV AND TGFCAB.IDIPROC = TPRIATV.IDIPROC) 	WHERE TGFCAB.IDIPROC = ?  	AND TGFITE.CODPROD = ?   	AND TGFITE.SEQUENCIA > 0  	AND TGFCAB.TIPMOV <> 'F'  GROUP BY TGFITE.CODPROD, TGFITE.CONTROLE, TGFEST.DTVAL, TPRIATV.IDEFX  ORDER BY IDEFX DESC, DTVAL ASC
